posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:Zhaoqing Phoenix Country Garden Hotel is located in the beautiful Zhaoqing, with beautiful surroundings and picturesque scenery. The hotel is surrounded by green trees and blooming flowers, as if you are in a natural oxygen bar. Whenever night falls, the night view of the hotel is even more beautiful, with bright lights, which complement the surrounding natural environment, forming a moving picture.
However, despite the pleasant scenery of the hotel, the condition of the room is somewhat unsatisfactory. Entering the room, the first thing that catches your eye is the slightly old decoration and furniture. The paint on the wall has begun to peel off, and some furniture has also shown signs of wear. Although the bed is clean and tidy, the elasticity of the mattress seems to have weakened, which makes people feel a little uncomfortable when sleeping. In addition, the facilities in the bathroom also look a bit old, and some equipment is not smooth to use.
